<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">CHICAGO,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="23x1" data-tblname="263812" data-tblv="10" id="led263812F202210161668633717688">October 5, 2023</a> &#8212; Today Conagra Brands, Inc. All comparisons are against the prior-year fiscal period, unless otherwise noted.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;"><b><u>CEO Perspective</u></b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;"><font style="color:#000000;">Sean Connolly, president and chief executive officer of Conagra Brands, commented, "I am proud of our team for delivering another quarter of strong margin recovery and EPS growth despite facing industry-wide macro dynamics that have affected consumer purchasing behavior and elongated the volume recovery period. We will continue to focus on executing our&nbsp;Conagra Way playbook as we make targeted and disciplined investments throughout the remainder of the year to drive the top-line. We are reaffirming our guidance for fiscal 2024, reflecting confidence in our plans, people and agility as we continue to navigate a shifting consumer environment."</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Total Company&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657299993307">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, net sales were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049165813">$2.9</a> billion reflecting:</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049248360">0.3%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049261993">increase</a> from the favorable impact of foreign exchange; and</p>
			</td>

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049334186">0.3%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049359561">decrease</a> in organic net sales was driven by a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049390922">6.6%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049403285">decrease</a> in volume largely&nbsp;due to industry-wide slowdown in consumption&nbsp;and recent consumer behavior shifts, partially offset by a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660049379536">6.3%</a> improvement in price/mix.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left;"><b>Page 2</b></p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Gross profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049499647">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049508835">14.3%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049519257">$823</a> million in the quarter, and adjusted gross profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049823859">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049833892">10.9%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049842458">$801</a> million.&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="55x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657300031982">First quarter</a> gross profit increased primarily as a result of inflation-driven pricing that was implemented in fiscal 2023 and productivity, which more than offset the negative impacts of cost of goods sold inflation,&nbsp;unfavorable operating leverage, and lower organic net sales.&nbsp;Gross margin&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049875311">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049885768">354</a> basis points to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="4x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049898776">28.3%</a> in the quarter, and adjusted gross margin&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049914074">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049924191">272</a> basis points to <a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049932524">27.6%</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Selling, general, and administrative expense (SG&amp;A), which includes advertising and promotional expense (A&amp;P),&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049962754">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049972518">54.9%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049981591">$334</a> million in the qu<font style="color:#333333;">arter due primarily to the goodwill and brand impairments that occurred in the prior year quarter. A</font>djusted SG&amp;A, which excludes A&amp;P,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660049996959">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050005761">1.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050019689">$258</a> million <font style="color:#000000;">driven by lower incentive compensation&nbsp;compared to&nbsp;the prior year quarter.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><font style="color:#000000;">A&amp;P for the quarter decreased 5.3%&nbsp;to</font><font style="color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050063043">$59</a><font style="color:#000000;"> million, driven primarily by timing of modern marketing initiatives.&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net interest expense was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F2022791660050151152">$106</a> million in the quarter. Compared to the prior-year period, net interest expense&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F2022791660050170543">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F2022791660050179416">9.2%</a> or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x3" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F2022791660050187647">$9</a> m<font style="color:#333333;">illion, primarily due to a higher weighted average interest rate on outstanding debt.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The average diluted share count in the quarter was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F2022791660050327584">480</a> million shares.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left;">In the quarter, net income attributable to Conagra Brands was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050393587">$320</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050408870">$0.67</a> per diluted share compared to a net loss of $0.16 per diluted share in the prior year quarter. Adjusted net income attributable to Conagra Brands&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660050427061">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660051208036">15.0%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660051216702">$316</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="14x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F2022791660051225596">$0.66</a> per diluted share. The increase was&nbsp;driven primarily by the increase in gross profit and decrease in SG&amp;A, as previously discussed.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Adjusted EBITDA, which includes equity method investment earnings and pension and postretirement non-service expense (income),&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="10" id="led263861F2022791660051274036">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="10" id="led263861F2022791660051283076">12.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="10" id="led263861F2022791660051294195">$613</a> million in the quarter, primarily driven by the increase&nbsp;in adjusted gross profit.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Grocery &amp; Snacks Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657299999539">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Grocery &amp; Snacks segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660051335237">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660051343571">1.2%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F2022791660051355324">$1.2</a> billion in the quarter&nbsp;driven by a&nbsp;price/mix increase of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="14x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660834530115">5.6%,</a>&nbsp;partially <font style="color:#000000;">offset by a volume decrease of&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="13x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660834559215">4.4%</a><font style="color:#000000;">&nbsp;from&nbsp;industry-wide consumption trends.&nbsp;In the quarter, the company gained dollar share in snacking categories including seeds and microwave popcorn, and some staples categories including chili and canned meat.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835300580">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835314034">3.3%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835328717">$259</a> million in the quarter. Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835351847">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835364347">3.8%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835378757">$264</a> million&nbsp;as higher organic net sales and productivity more than offset the negative impacts of cost of goods sold inflation, unfavorable operating leverage, and&nbsp;higher A&amp;P and SG&amp;A.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Refrigerated &amp; Frozen Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657300003588">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Refrigerated &amp; Frozen segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663088117935">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663088127664">4.6%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663088149020">$1.2</a> billion in th<font style="color:#000000;">e quarter due to a volume&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="18x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845828718">decrease</a><font style="color:#000000;">&nbsp;of&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="18x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845838199">10.5%&nbsp;</a><font style="color:#000000;">from&nbsp;industry-wide&nbsp;consumption trends, partially offset by a price mix&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="19x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845796630">increase</a><font style="color:#000000;">&nbsp;of&nbsp;</font><a data-tblloc="19x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845814175">5.9%</a><font style="color:#000000;">.&nbsp;In the quarter, the company gained dollar share in categories such as frozen sides and&nbsp;frozen breakfast sausage.</font></p>

Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835439908">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835449131">14.7%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835460673">$201</a> million as productivity and lower A&amp;P more than offset the negative impacts of lower organic net sales,&nbsp;unfavorable operating leverage, cost of goods sold inflation, and increased&nbsp;SG&amp;A.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net sales for the International segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663087917870">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663087940696">11.4%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20228131663087957030">$260</a> million in the quarter reflecting:</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835480363">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835491457">12.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835507368">$24</a> million in the quarter primarily due to certain non-cash restructuring charges. Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835520838">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835529870">57.8%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835541056">$42</a> million as the benefits from higher organic net sales and&nbsp;productivity&nbsp;more than offset the negative impact&nbsp;of cost of goods sold inflation,&nbsp;unfavorable operating leverage, and higher SG&amp;A.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Foodservice Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657300012778">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Foodservice segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845944550">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845955102">5.2%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660845972046">$289</a> million in the quarter. Price/mix increased&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="30x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660846051858">10.3%</a>&nbsp;and volume&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="29x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660846017711">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="29x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="10" id="led263825F20227181660846029439">5.1%</a>primarily from&nbsp;the elasticity impact of the company's inflation-driven pricing actions.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835595723">$44</a> million compared to $1 million in the prior year quarter.&nbsp;Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835613611">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835622376">87.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20227181660835631690">$41</a> million in the quarter as the benefits of higher organic net sales and productivity more than offset the impacts of cost of goods sold inflation&nbsp;and unfavorable operating leverage.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Other&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="10" id="led263810F2022681657300016886">First Quarter</a> Items</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Corporate expenses&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089724781">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089737077">56.0%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089748565">$37</a> million in the qua<font style="color:#333333;">rter and adjuste</font>d corporate expense&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089764461">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089773144">20.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="10" id="led263837F20228131663089783848">$64</a> million in the<font style="color:#333333;"> quarter driven primarily by lower incentive compensation compared to&nbsp;the prior year quarter.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Pension and post-retirement non-service expense was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F20227181660846326307">$0</a>&nbsp;compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x2" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F20227181660846339340">$6</a> million of income in the prior-year period due primarily to higher interest costs.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, equity method investment earnings decreased 27.9% to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="10" id="led263814F20227181660846351987">$36</a> million as results from the company's joint venture, Ardent Mills, reflected&nbsp;slightly lower volume trends in the milling industry.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, the effective tax rate was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F20227181660846611717">23.5%</a> compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x2" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F20227181660846626747">(22.8)%</a> in the prior-year period. The adjusted effective tax rate was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F20227181660846645523">23.6%</a> compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x2" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="10" id="led263848F20227181660846654756">22.9%</a> in the prior-year period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, the company<font style="color:#333333;"> paid a dividend of $0.33&nbsp;per share.&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Outlook</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The company is reiterating its fiscal 2024 outlook and&nbsp;providing high-level drivers for the second quarter and back half of the year. For the second quarter, the company is expecting a low-single digit organic net sales decline as volume declines improve as inflation-driven pricing actions from fiscal 2023 are wrapped. We expect&nbsp;gross and operating margins to be below the first quarter due to incremental trade and A&amp;P investment. For the back half of the year, the company is expecting low-single digit organic net sales growth driven by year-over-year&nbsp;volume growth, along with margins similar to Q2 as trade and A&amp;P dollars remain elevated.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Discussion of Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Conagra Brands will host a webcast and conference call at 9:30 a.m. Eastern time today to discuss the results. The live audio webcast and presentation slides will be available on <u>www.conagrabrands.com/investor-relations</u> under Events &amp; Presentations. The conference call may be accessed by dialing 1-877-883-0383 for participants in the U.S. and 1-412-902-6506 for all other participants and using passcode 4734297. Please dial in 10 to 15 minutes prior to the call start time. Following the company's remarks, the conference call will include a question-and-answer session with the investment community. A replay of the webcast will be available on www.conagrabrands.com/investor-relations under Events &amp; Presentations until October 5, 2024.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About Conagra Brands</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Conagra Brands, Inc. (NYSE: CAG), headquartered in Chicago, is one of North America's leading branded food companies. Guided by an entrepreneurial spirit, Conagra Brands combines a rich heritage of making great food with a sharpened focus on innovation. The company's portfolio is evolving to satisfy people's changing food preferences. Conagra's iconic brands, such as Birds Eye&#174;, Duncan Hines&#174;, Healthy Choice&#174;, Marie&nbsp;Callender's&#174;, Reddi-wip&#174;, and&nbsp;Slim Jim&#174;, as well as emerging brands, including Angie's&#174; BOOMCHICKAPOP&#174;, Duke's&#174;, Earth Balance&#174;, Gardein&#174;, and Frontera&#174;, offer choices for every occasion. For more information, visit <u>www.conagrabrands.com</u>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Note on Forward-Looking Statements</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">This document contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws. These forward-looking statements are based on management's current expectations and are subject to uncertainty and changes in circumstances. Readers of this document should understand that these statements are not guarantees of performance or results. Many factors could affect our actual financial results and cause them to vary materially from the expectations contained in the forward-looking statements, including those set forth in this document. These risks, uncertainties, and factors include, among other things: risks associated with general economic and industry conditions, including inflation, rising interest rates, decreased availability of capital, volatility in financial markets, declining consumer spending rates, recessions, decreased energy availability, increased energy costs (including fuel surcharges), supply chain challenges, labor shortages, and geopolitical conflicts (including the ongoing conflict between Russia and Ukraine); negative impacts caused by public health crises; risks related to our ability to deleverage on currently anticipated timelines, and to continue to access capital on acceptable terms or at all; risks related to the company's competitive environment, cost structure, and related market conditions; risks related to our ability to execute operating and value creation plans and achieve returns on our investments and targeted operating efficiencies from cost-saving initiatives, and to benefit from trade optimization programs; risks related to the availability and prices of commodities and other supply chain resources, including raw materials, packaging, energy, and transportation, including any negative effects caused by changes in levels of inflation and interest rates, weather conditions, health pandemics or outbreaks of disease, actual or threatened hostilities or war, or other geopolitical uncertainty; risks related to the effectiveness of our hedging activities and ability to respond to volatility in commodities; disruptions or inefficiencies in our supply chain and/or operations; risks related to the ultimate impact of, including reputational harm caused by, any product recalls and product liability or labeling litigation, including litigation related to lead-based paint and pigment and cooking spray; risks related to our ability to respond to changing consumer preferences and the success of our innovation and marketing investments; risks associated with actions by our customers, including changes in distribution and purchasing terms; risks related to the seasonality of our business; risks associated with our co-manufacturing arrangements and other third-party service provider dependencies; risks associated with actions of governments and regulatory bodies that affect our businesses, including the ultimate impact of new or revised regulations or interpretations including to address climate change or implement changes to taxes and tariffs; risks related to the company's ability to execute on its strategies or achieve expectations related to environmental, social, and governance matters, including as a result of evolving legal, regulatory, and other standards, processes, and assumptions, the pace of scientific and technological developments, increased costs, the availability of requisite financing, and changes in carbon pricing or carbon taxes; risks related to a material failure in or breach of our or our vendors' information technology systems and other cybersecurity incidents; risks related to our ability to identify, attract, hire, train, retain and develop qualified personnel; risk of increased pension, labor or people-related expenses; risks and uncertainties associated with intangible assets, including any future goodwill or intangible assets impairment charges; risk relating to our ability to protect our intellectual property rights; risks relating to acquisition, divestiture, joint venture or investment activities; the amount and timing of future dividends, which remain subject to Board approval and depend on market and other conditions; and other risks described in our reports filed from time to time&nbsp;with the Securities and Exchange Commission.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">We caution readers not to place undue reliance on any forward-looking statements included in this document, which speak only as of the date of this document. We undertake no responsibility to update these statements, except as required by law.</p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Note on Non-GAAP Financial Measures</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">This document includes certain non-GAAP financial measures, including adjusted EPS, organic net sales, adjusted gross profit, adjusted operating profit, adjusted SG&amp;A, adjusted corporate expenses, adjusted gross margin, adjusted operating margin, adjusted effective tax rate, adjusted net income attributable to Conagra Brands, free cash flow, net debt, net leverage ratio, and adjusted EBITDA. Management considers GAAP financial measures as well as such non-GAAP financial information in its evaluation of the company&#8217;s financial statements and believes these non-GAAP financial measures provide useful supplemental information to assess the company&#8217;s operating performance and financial position. These measures should be viewed in addition to, and not in lieu of, the company&#8217;s diluted earnings per share, operating performance and financial measures as calculated in accordance with GAAP.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Organic net sales excludes, from reported net sales, the impacts of foreign exchange, divested businesses and acquisitions, as well as the impact of any 53<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">rd</sup> week. All references to changes in volume and price/mix throughout this release are on an organic net sales basis.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">References to adjusted items throughout this release refer to measures computed in accordance with GAAP less the impact of items impacting comparability. Items impacting comparability are income or expenses (and related tax impacts) that management believes have had, or are likely to have, a significant impact on the earnings of the applicable business segment or on the total corporation for the period in which the item is recognized, and are not indicative of the company&#8217;s core operating results. These items thus affect the comparability of underlying results from period to period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">References to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (EBITDA) refer to net income attributable to Conagra Brands before the impacts of discontinued operations, income tax expense (benefit), interest expense, depreciation, and amortization. References to adjusted EBITDA refer to EBITDA before the impacts of items impacting comparability.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Hedge gains and losses are generally aggregated, and net amounts are reclassified from unallocated corporate expense to the operating segments when the underlying commodity or foreign currency being hedged is expensed in segment cost of goods sold. The net change in the derivative gains (losses) included in unallocated corporate expense during the period is reflected as a comparability item, Corporate hedging derivate gains (losses).</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Note on Forward-Looking&nbsp;Non-GAAP Financial Measures</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Our fiscal 2024 guidance includes certain non-GAAP financial measures (organic net sales growth, adjusted operating margin, adjusted EPS, net leverage ratio, and adjusted effective tax rate) that are presented on a forward-looking basis. Historically, the company has calculated these non-GAAP financial measures excluding the impact of certain items such as, but not limited to, foreign exchange, acquisitions, divestitures, restructuring expenses, the extinguishment of debt, hedging gains and losses, impairment charges, legacy legal contingencies, and unusual tax items. Reconciliations of these forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures are not provided because the company is unable to provide such reconciliations without unreasonable effort, due to the uncertainty and inherent difficulty of predicting the timing and financial impact of such items. For the same reasons, the company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information, which could be material to future results.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">1 </sup>Operating profit is derived from taking Income from continuing operations before income taxes and equity method investment earnings, adding back Interest expense, net and removing Pension and postretirement non-service income.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">2</sup> Advertising and promotion expense (A&amp;P) has been removed from adjusted selling, general and administrative expense because this metric is used in reporting to management, and management believes this adjusted measure provides useful supplemental information to assess the company&#8217;s operating performance.&nbsp; Please note that A&amp;P is not removed from adjusted profit measures.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">3&nbsp;</sup>In Q1 FY23, we reported a GAAP net loss. In periods when we recognize a net loss, we exclude the impact of outstanding stock awards from the diluted loss per share calculation, as their inclusion would have an anti-dilutive effect. The adjusted diluted earnings per share calculation includes the impact of outstanding stock awards.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;">4 </sup>The company defines its net debt leverage ratio as net debt divided by adjusted EBITDA for the trailing twelve month period.</p>

e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
